plane-crazy 2021-08-08 10:17:45 Gravity in roblox is 196.2 studs/s^2 (print(workspace.Gravity)
Gravity on earth is ~9.81 meters/s^2

(196.2stud/s^2) / (9.81 * meter/s^2) = 20stud/meter

That is where the widely quoted 20 studs/meter come from.
